Global hi!

This November we are having Alias game tournament among Innopolis companies (Alias is a game, where you have to describe some word with other words. Very close to "Salad bowl" game)

Limits:
- 4 players per team
- Any amount of command from each innopolis company
- Ru and En leagues (you can compete in both, if your team plans to compete in both)

Teams registration proceeds up to the 1st of November (Registration start will be declared later)

Event channel:
https://t.me/innoalias
